Task instruction sent to agent 
# Task: Implement PolicyQuotaController for Cilium

## Objective
Create a `PolicyQuotaController` in Cilium that enforces per-namespace limits on the
number of `CiliumNetworkPolicy` resources, preventing policy sprawl in multi-tenant clusters.

## Requirements

1. **Create `pkg/policy/quota/controller.go`** with:
   - `PolicyQuotaController` struct that watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
   - `NewPolicyQuotaController(client, informer, maxPerNamespace int)` constructor
   - `Run(ctx context.Context)` method implementing the controller loop
   - Per-namespace counting using a thread-safe map
   - `CheckQuota(namespace string) error` method that returns error if quota exceeded

2. **Create CRD type** `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_policy_quota.go`:
   - `CiliumPolicyQuota` struct with `Spec.MaxPoliciesPerNamespace` field
   - Follow existing Cilium CRD patterns (DeepCopy, runtime.Object)

3. **Create `pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go`** with tests

4. **Follow Cilium patterns**:
   - Use `hive` dependency injection framework
   - Use `resource.Resource[T]` for watching K8s resources
   - Use `logfields` for structured logging

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/policy/k8s/watcher.go` — CiliumNetworkPolicy watcher pattern
- `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_cnp.go` — CiliumNetworkPolicy CRD type
- `operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/` — controller using hive pattern
- `pkg/k8s/resource/resource.go` — resource watching framework

## Success Criteria
- PolicyQuotaController struct with Run method exists
- CheckQuota method performs namespace counting
- CiliumPolicyQuota CRD type exists
- Uses Cilium's hive/resource patterns
- Test file exists with test functions

    33→// Resource provides access to a Kubernetes resource through either
    34→// a stream of events or a read-only store.
    35→//
    36→// Observing of the events can be done from a constructor as subscriber
    37→// registration is non-blocking.
    38→//
    39→// Store() however should only be called from a start hook, or from a
    40→// goroutine forked from the start hook as it blocks until the store
    41→// has been synchronized.
    42→//
    43→// The subscriber can process the events from Events() asynchronously and in
    44→// parallel, but for each event the Done() function must be called to mark
    45→// the event as handled. If not done no new events will be emitted for this key.
    46→// If an event handling is marked as failed the configured error handler is called
    4

    27→	scopedLog := r.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{
    28→		logfields.Controller: "ciliumenvoyconfig",
    29→		logfields.Resource:   req.NamespacedName,
    30→	})

    32→
    33→	svc := &corev1.Service{}
    34→	if err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, svc); err != nil {
    35→		if k8serrors.IsNotFound(err) {
    36→			scopedLog.WithError(err).Debug("Unable to get service - either deleted or not yet available")
    37→			return ctrl.Result{}, nil
    38→		}
    39→
    40→		return ctrl.Result{}, err
    41→	}
    42→
    43→	if isLBProtocolAnnotationEnabled(svc) || hasAnyPort(svc, r.ports) {
    44→		if err := r.createOrUpdateEnvoyConfig(ctx, svc); err != nil {
    45→			return ctrl.Result{}, err
    46→		}
    47→	} else {
    48→		if err := r.deleteEnvoyConfig(ctx, svc); err != nil {
    49→			return ctrl.Result{}, err
    50→		}
    51→	}
    52→

     4→// Package logfields defines common logging fields which are used across packages
     5→package logfields
     6→
     7→const (
     8→	// Annotations are any annotations for Pods
     9→	Annotations = "annotations"
    10→
    11→	// LogSubsys is the field denoting the subsystem when logging

# Simplify: Code Review and Cleanup

Review all changed files for reuse, quality, and efficiency. Fix any issues found.

## Phase 1: Identify Changes

Run `git diff` (or `git diff HEAD` if there are staged changes) to see what changed. If there are no git changes, review the most recently modified files that the user mentioned or that you edited earlier in this conversation.

## Phase 2: Launch Three Review Agents in Parallel

Use the Agent tool to launch all three agents concurrently in a single message. Pass each agent the full diff so it has the complete context.

### Agent 1: Code Reuse Review

For each change:

1. **Search for existing utilities and helpers** that could replace newly written code. Use Grep to find similar patterns elsewhere in the codebase — common locations are utility directories, shared modules, and files adjacent to the changed ones.
2. **Flag any new function that duplicates existing functionality.** Suggest the existing function to use instead.

	events chan resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]
}

// Events returns the channel of resource events

	return m.events
}

// SendEvent is a helper to send events through the mock resource
func (m *MockResource) SendEvent(event resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]) {
	m.events <- event
}

// CloseEvents closes the event channel
func (m *MockResource) CloseEvents() {
	close(m.events)
}

	return &MockResource{
		events: make(chan resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy], 100),
	}
}

  - Properly calls `event.Done(err)` for event acknowledgment

  - `policyCounts`: Per-namespace policy counts
  - `policyKeys`: Tracks which policies have been counted (prevents double-counting on updates)
  - `sync.RWMutex` for thread-safe access

  - `onPolicyUpsert()`: Increments count only on new policies
  - `onPolicyDelete()`: Decrements count and cleans up empty namespaces

&types.SlimCNP{\n\t\t\t\t\tCiliumNetworkPolicy: &cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tTypeMeta:   event.Object.TypeMeta,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tObjectMeta: event.Object.ObjectMeta,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tSpec:       event.Object.Spec,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tSpecs:      event.Object.Specs,\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tresourceID := ipcacheTypes.NewResourceID(\n\t\t\t\t\tipcacheTypes.ResourceKindCNP,\n\t\t\t\t\tslimCNP.ObjectMeta.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\t\tslimCNP.ObjectMeta.Name,\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\t\terr = p.onUpsert(slimCNP, event.Key, k8sAPIGroupCiliumNetworkPolicyV2, resourceID)\n\t\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\t\terr = p.onDelete(slimCNP, event.Key, k8sAPIGroupCiliumNetworkPolicyV2, resourceID)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treportCNPChangeMetrics(err)\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t// Exit when all channels closed\n\t\t\tif knpEvents == nil && cnpEvents == nil && ccnpEvents == nil && ... {\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n}\n```\n\n**Key Patterns:**\n- Uses `resource.Resource[T]` to get event channels\n- `resource.Events(ctx)` returns `<-chan resource.Event[T]`\n- Event types: `resource.Sync`, `resource.Upsert`, `resource.Delete`\n- **Critical:** Must call `event.Done(err)` for each event - failure means no new events for that key\n- Sync events mark initial listing complete\n- Create intermediate representations (SlimCNP) when needed\n- Use atomic.Bool for synchronization flags\n\n---\n\n### 3. Resource.Resource[T] Pattern (pkg/k8s/resource/resource.go)\n\n**File:** `/workspace/pkg/k8s/resource/resource.go` (key excerpts)\n\n```go\n// Resource[T] interface - the core abstraction\ntype Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\n\t// Observable interface (from stream.Observable)\n\tstream.Observable[Event[T]]\n\n\t// Events returns channel of events\n\t// Each event MUST be marked as handled with Done()\n\t// Missing Done() causes panic via finalizer\n\t//\n\t// Event sequence:\n\t// (start), Upsert*, Upsert*, (done replaying), Upsert, Upsert,\n\t//   (synced), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\n\tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\n\n\t// Store retrieves read-only store, blocks until synchronized\n\tStore(context.Context) (Store[T], error)\n}\n\n// Constructor function\nfunc New[T k8sRuntime.Object](\n\tlc cell.Lifecycle,\n\tlw cache.ListerWatcher,\n\topts ...ResourceOption,\n) Resource[T] {\n\tr := &resource[T]{lw: lw}\n\tr.opts.sourceObj = func() k8sRuntime.Object {\n\t\tvar obj T\n\t\treturn obj\n\t}\n\tfor _, o := range opts {\n\t\to(&r.opts)\n\t}\n\tr.ctx, r.cancel = context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n\tr.reset()\n\tlc.Append(r)\n\treturn r\n}\n\n// ResourceOption patterns - functional options\nfunc WithTransform[From, To k8sRuntime.Object](\n\ttransform func(From) (To, error),\n) ResourceOption {\n\treturn WithLazyTransform(\n\t\tfunc() k8sRuntime.Object {\n\t\t\tvar obj From\n\t\t\treturn obj\n\t\t},\n\t\tfunc(fromRaw any) (any, error) {\n\t\t\tif from, ok := fromRaw.(From); ok {\n\t\t\t\tto, err := transform(from)\n\t\t\t\treturn to, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"expected %T, got %T\", nil, fromRaw)\n\t\t})\n}\n\nfunc WithMetric(scope string) ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.metricScope = scope\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithIndexers(indexers cache.Indexers) ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.indexers = indexers\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithName(name string) ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.name = name\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithStoppableInformer() ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.releasable = true\n\t}\n}\n\n// Event structure\ntype Event[T k8sRuntime.Object] struct {\n\tKind   EventKind  // Sync, Upsert, or Delete\n\tKey    Key        // resource.Key{Namespace, Name}\n\tObject T          // The actual object\n\tDone   func(error) // Must call when handled\n}\n\n// EventKind enum\nconst (\n\tSync EventKind   // Initial sync complete\n\tUpsert EventKind // Create or update\n\tDelete EventKind // Deletion\n)\n\n// Event options for tuning retry behavior\nfunc WithRateLimiter(r workqueue.RateLimiter) EventsOpt {\n\treturn func(o *eventsOpts) {\n\t\to.rateLimiter = r\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithErrorHandler(h ErrorHandler) EventsOpt {\n\treturn func(o *eventsOpts) {\n\t\to.errorHandler = h\n\t}\n}\n\n// ErrorHandler signature\n// (key, retryCount, error) -> ErrorAction\ntype ErrorHandler func(Key, int, error) ErrorAction\n\n// Default behavior: AlwaysRetry\nconst (\n\tErrorActionRetry  ErrorAction\n\tErrorActionStop   ErrorAction\n\tErrorActionIgnore ErrorAction\n)\n```\n\n**Usage Example:**\n```go\n// In a hive cell/constructor\nvar exampleCell = hive.Module(\n\t\"example\",\n\tcell.Provide(\n\t\tfunc(lc cell.Lifecycle, c k8sClient.Clientset) resource.Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod] {\n\t\t\tlw := utils.ListerWatcherFromTyped[*slim_corev1.PodList](\n\t\t\t\tc.Slim().CoreV1().Pods(\"\"),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t\treturn resource.New(\n\t\t\t\tlc, lw,\n\t\t\t\tresource.WithMetric(\"pods\"),\n\t\t\t\tresource.WithName(\"pods\"),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t},\n\t),\n)\n\n// Consuming the resource\nfunc usePods(pods resource.Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod]) {\n\tgo func() {\n\t\tfor event := range pods.Events(ctx) {\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\t// Initial sync complete\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\terr := onPodUpsert(event.Object)\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\terr := onPodDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n}\n\n// Or use the store directly (blocks until synced)\nstore, err := pods.Store(ctx)\nallPods := store.List()\n```\n\n**Key Patterns:**\n- Lazy initialization (informer only starts when Events() or Store() called)\n- **CRITICAL:** Must call `event.Done(error)` - missing it causes panic via finalizer\n- Sync event signals initial replay of existing objects complete\n- Functional options for configuration\n- Support for object transformation (e.g., SlimCNP from full CNP)\n- Rate limiting and error handling for retries\n- Metrics collection support\n\n---\n\n### 4. Hive Cell Pattern for Controllers (operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/)\n\n**File:** `/workspace/operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/cell.go`\n\n```go\n// Cell is the hive module definition\nvar Cell = cell.Module(\n\t\"ciliumenvoyconfig\",\n\t\"Manages the CiliumEnvoyConfig controllers\",\n\n\t// Configuration structure with flags\n\tcell.Config(l7LoadBalancerConfig{\n\t\tLoadBalancerL7:          \"\",\n\t\tLoadBalancerL7Ports:     []string{},\n\t\tLoadBalancerL7Algorithm: \"round_robin\",\n\t}),\n\t\n\t// Register the controller setup function\n\tcell.Invoke(registerL7LoadBalancingController),\n)\n\n// Configuration structure with pflag.FlagSet integration\ntype l7LoadBalancerConfig struct {\n\tLoadBalancerL7          string\n\tLoadBalancerL7Algorithm string\n\tLoadBalancerL7Ports     []string\n}\n\nfunc (r l7LoadBalancerConfig) Flags(flags *pflag.FlagSet) {\n\tflags.String(\"loadbalancer-l7\", r.LoadBalancerL7, \n\t\t\"Enable L7 loadbalancer capabilities for services via L7 proxy. Applicable values: envoy\")\n\tflags.String(\"loadbalancer-l7-algorithm\", r.LoadBalancerL7Algorithm, \n\t\t\"Default LB algorithm for services that do not specify related annotation\")\n\tflags.StringSlice(\"loadbalancer-l7-ports\", r.LoadBalancerL7Ports, \n\t\t\"List of service ports that will be automatically redirected to backend.\")\n}\n\n// Parameter injection using cell.In\ntype l7LoadbalancerParams struct {\n\tcell.In\n\n\tLogger             logrus.FieldLogger\n\tCtrlRuntimeManager ctrlRuntime.Manager\n\tConfig             l7LoadBalancerConfig\n}\n\n// Invoke function - runs during hive startup\nfunc registerL7LoadBalancingController(params l7LoadbalancerParams) error {\n\tif params.Config.LoadBalancerL7 != \"envoy\" {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tparams.Logger.Info(\"Register Envoy load balancer reconciler\")\n\n\treconciler := newCiliumEnvoyConfigReconciler(\n\t\tparams.CtrlRuntimeManager.GetClient(),\n\t\tparams.Logger,\n\t\tparams.Config.LoadBalancerL7Algorithm,\n\t\tparams.Config.LoadBalancerL7Ports,\n\t\t10,\n\t\toperatorOption.Config.ProxyIdleTimeoutSeconds,\n\t)\n\n\tif err := reconciler.SetupWithManager(params.CtrlRuntimeManager); err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to setup Envoy load balancer reconciler: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n```\n\n**File:** `/workspace/operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/ciliumenvoyconfig.go`\n\n```go\n// Reconciler struct - implements controller-runtime Reconciler interface\ntype ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler struct {\n\tclient client.Client\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger\n\n\talgorithm          string\n\tports              []string\n\tmaxRetries         int\n\tidleTimeoutSeconds int\n}\n\nfunc newCiliumEnvoyConfigReconciler(\n\tc client.Client,\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger,\n\tdefaultAlgorithm string,\n\tports []string,\n\tmaxRetries int,\n\tidleTimeoutSeconds int,\n) *ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler {\n\treturn &ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler{\n\t\tclient: c,\n\t\tlogger: logger,\n\t\talgorithm: defaultAlgorithm,\n\t\tports: ports,\n\t\tmaxRetries: maxRetries,\n\t\tidleTimeoutSeconds: idleTimeoutSeconds,\n\t}\n}\n\n// SetupWithManager - called from hive to register with controller-runtime\nfunc (r *ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {\n\treturn ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).\n\t\tFor(&corev1.Service{}).        // Watch Service resources\n\t\tOwns(&ciliumv2.CiliumEnvoyConfig{}). // Own CiliumEnvoyConfig resources\n\t\tComplete(r)                     // Install this as the reconciler\n}\n\n// Reconcile - the core reconciliation loop (implements controller-runtime Reconciler)\nfunc (r *ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler) Reconcile(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\treq ctrl.Request,\n) (ctrl.Result, error) {\n\t// Create scoped logger with context\n\tscopedLog := r.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Controller: \"ciliumenvoyconfig\",\n\t\tlogfields.Resource:   req.NamespacedName,\n\t})\n\tscopedLog.Info(\"Starting reconciliation\")\n\n\tsvc := &corev1.Service{}\n\tif err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, svc); err != nil {\n\t\tif k8serrors.IsNotFound(err) {\n\t\t\tscopedLog.WithError(err).Debug(\"Unable to get service - either deleted or not yet available\")\n\t\t\treturn ctrl.Result{}, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn ctrl.Result{}, err\n\t}\n\n\tif isLBProtocolAnnotationEnabled(svc) || hasAnyPort(svc, r.ports) {\n\t\tif err := r.createOrUpdateEnvoyConfig(ctx, svc); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn ctrl.Result{}, err\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tif err := r.deleteEnvoyConfig(ctx, svc); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn ctrl.Result{}, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog.Info(\"Successfully reconciled\")\n\treturn ctrl.Result{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Key Patterns:**\n- `cell.Module()` declares a hive module with name and description\n- `cell.Config()` registers configuration struct with automatic flag binding\n- Configuration type must implement `Flags(*pflag.FlagSet)` method\n- `cell.Invoke()` registers setup functions that run during hive startup\n- Parameter injection via `cell.In` struct tag for dependency injection\n- Reconciler implements `Reconcile(context.Context, ctrl.Request)` method\n- `SetupWithManager()` configures the controller:\n  - `For(&resource)` - watches primary resource\n  - `Owns(&resource)` - watches owned resources\n  - `Complete(reconciler)` - registers the reconciler\n- Controller-runtime auto-enqueues updates when watched resources change\n\n---\n\n### 5. Only object keys are queued and if an object is changed multiple times\n   438\u2192// before the subscriber can handle the event only the latest state of object\n   439\u2192// is emitted.\n   440\u2192//\n   441\u2192// The 'ctx' is used to cancel the subscription. The returned channel will be\n   442\u2192// closed when context is cancelled.\n   443\u2192//\n   444\u2192// Options are supported to configure rate limiting of retries\n   445\u2192// (WithRateLimiter), error handling strategy (WithErrorHandler).\n   446\u2192//\n   447\u2192// By default all errors are retried, the default rate limiter of workqueue\n   448\u2192// package is used and the channel is unbuffered.\n   449\u2192func (r *resource[T]) Events(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T] {\n   450\u2192\t_, callerFile, callerLine, _ := runtime.Caller(1)\n   451\u2192\tdebugInfo := fmt.Sprintf(\"%T.Events() called from %s:%d\", r, callerFile, callerLine)\n   452\u2192\n   453\u2192\toptions := eventsOpts{\n   454\u2192\t\terrorHandler: AlwaysRetry, // Default error handling is to always retry.\n   455\u2192\t\trateLimiter:  workqueue.DefaultControllerRateLimiter(),\n   456\u2192\t}\n   457\u2192\tfor _, apply := range opts {\n   458\u2192\t\tapply(&options)\n   459\u2192\t}\n   460\u2192\n   461\u2192\t// Mark the resource as needed. This will start the informer if it was not already.\n   462\u2192\tr.markNeeded()\n   463\u2192\n   464\u2192\tout := make(chan Event[T])\n   465\u2192\tctx, subCancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n   466\u2192\n   467\u2192\tsub := &subscriber[T]{\n   468\u2192\t\tr:         r,\n   469\u2192\t\toptions:   options,\n   470\u2192\t\tdebugInfo: debugInfo,\n   471\u2192\t\twq: workqueue.NewRateLimitingQueueWithConfig(options.rateLimiter,\n   472\u2192\t\t\tworkqueue.RateLimitingQueueConfig{Name: r.resourceName()}),\n   473\u2192\t}\n   474\u2192\n   475\u2192\t// Fork a goroutine to process the queued keys and pass them to the subscriber.\n   476\u2192\tr.wg.Add(1)\n   477\u2192\tgo func() {\n   478\u2192\t\tdefer r.release()\n   479\u2192\t\tdefer r.wg.Done()\n   480\u2192\t\tdefer close(out)\n   481\u2192\n   482\u2192\t\t// Grab a handle to the store. Asynchronous as informer is started in the background.\n   483\u2192\t\tstore, err := r.storePromise.Await(ctx)\n   484\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n   485\u2192\t\t\t// Subscriber cancelled before the informer started, bail out.\n   486\u2192\t\t\treturn\n   487\u2192\t\t}\n   488\u2192\n   489\u2192\t\tr.mu.Lock()\n   490\u2192\t\tsubId := r.subId\n   491\u2192\t\tr.subId++\n   492\u2192\t\tr.subscribers[subId] = sub\n   493\u2192\n   494\u2192\t\t// Populate the queue with the initial set of keys that are already\n   495\u2192\t\t// in the store. Done under the resource lock to synchronize with delta\n   496\u2192\t\t// processing to make sure we don't end up queuing the key as initial key,\n   497\u2192\t\t// processing it and then requeuing it again.\n   498\u2192\t\tinitialKeys := store.IterKeys()\n   499\u2192\t\tfor initialKeys.Next() {\n   500\u2192\t\t\tsub.enqueueKey(initialKeys.Key())\n   501\u2192\t\t}\n   502\u2192\n   503\u2192\t\t// If the informer is already synchronized, then the above set of keys is a consistent\n   504\u2192\t\t// snapshot and we can queue the sync entry. If we're not yet synchronized the sync will\n   505\u2192\t\t// be queued from startWhenNeeded() after the informer has synchronized.\n   506\u2192\t\tif r.synchronized {\n   507\u2192\t\t\tsub.enqueueSync()\n   508\u2192\t\t}\n   509\u2192\t\tr.mu.Unlock()\n   510\u2192\n   511\u2192\t\tsub.processLoop(ctx, out, store)\n   512\u2192\n   513\u2192\t\tr.mu.Lock()\n   514\u2192\t\tdelete(r.subscribers, subId)\n   515\u2192\t\tr.mu.Unlock()\n   516\u2192\t}()\n   517\u2192\n   518\u2192\t// Fork a goroutine to wait for either the subscriber cancelling or the resource\n   519\u2192\t// shutting down.\n   520\u2192\tr.wg.Add(1)\n   521\u2192\tgo func() {\n   522\u2192\t\tdefer r.wg.Done()\n   523\u2192\t\tselect {\n   524\u2192\t\tcase <-r.ctx.Done():\n   525\u2192\t\tcase <-r.resetCtx.Done():\n   526\u2192\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   527\u2192\t\t}\n   528\u2192\t\tsubCancel()\n   529\u2192\t\tsub.wq.ShutDownWithDrain()\n   530\u2192\t}()\n   531\u2192\n   532\u2192\treturn out\n   533\u2192}\n   534\u2192\n   535\u2192func (r *resource[T]) release() {\n   536\u2192\tif !r.opts.releasable {\n   537\u2192\t\treturn\n   538\u2192\t}\n   539\u2192\n   540\u2192\t// in case of a releasable resource, stop the underlying informer when the last\n   541\u2192\t// reference to it is released. Calling ShutDownWithDrain is not\n   596\u2192\t// enough as DelayingQueue does not implement it, so without ShutDown() we'd\n   597\u2192\t// leak the (*delayingType).waitingLoop.\n   598\u2192\tdefer s.wq.ShutDown()\n   599\u2192\n   600\u2192\tdoneFinalizer := func(done *bool) {\n   601\u2192\t\t// If you get here it is because an Event[T] was handed to a subscriber\n   602\u2192\t\t// that forgot to call Event[T].Done().\n   603\u2192\t\t//\n   604\u2192\t\t// Calling Done() is needed to mark the event as handled. This allows\n   605\u2192\t\t// the next event for the same key to be handled and is used to clear\n   606\u2192\t\t// rate limiting and retry counts of prior failures.\n   607\u2192\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\n   608\u2192\t\t\t\"%s has a broken event handler that did not call Done() \"+\n   609\u2192\t\t\t\t\"before event was garbage collected\",\n   610\u2192\t\t\ts.debugInfo))\n   611\u2192\t}\n   612\u2192\n   613\u2192\t// To synthesize delete events to the subscriber we keep track of the last know state\n   614\u2192\t// of the object given to the subscriber. Objects are cleaned from this map when delete\n   615\u2192\t// events are successfully processed.\n   616\u2192\tvar lastKnownObjects lastKnownObjects[T]\n   617\u2192\n   618\u2192loop:\n   619\u2192\tfor {\n   620\u2192\t\t// Retrieve an item from the subscribers queue and then fetch the object\n   621\u2192\t\t// from the store.\n   622\u2192\t\tworkItem, shutdown := s.getWorkItem()\n   623\u2192\t\tif shutdown {\n   624\u2192\t\t\tbreak\n   625\u2192\t\t}\n   626\u2192\n   627\u2192\t\tvar event Event[T]\n   628\u2192\n   629\u2192\t\tswitch workItem := workItem.(type) {\n   630\u2192\t\tcase syncWorkItem:\n   631\u2192\t\t\tevent.Kind = Sync\n   632\u2192\t\tcase keyWorkItem:\n   633\u2192\t\t\tobj, exists, err := store.GetByKey(workItem.key)\n   634\u2192\t\t\tif !exists || err != nil {\n   635\u2192\t\t\t\t// The object no longer exists in the store and thus has been deleted.\n   636\u2192\t\t\t\tdeletedObject, ok := lastKnownObjects.Load(workItem.key)\n   637\u2192\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n   638\u2192\t\t\t\t\t// Object was never seen by the subscriber. newCount > c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\tscopedLog.Warn(\"Policy quota exceeded for namespace\")\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"policy quota exceeded: namespace %s has %d policies, max is %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, newCount, c.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog.Debug(\"Policy counted in namespace\")\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// onPolicyDelete handles policy deletion events.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyDelete(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tnamespace := policy.GetNamespace()\n\tname := policy.GetName()\n\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tif count, exists := policy quota.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tcount := c.policyCounts[namespace]\n\tc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif count >= c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"policy quota exceeded: namespace %s has %d policies, max is %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, count, c.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GetPolicyCounts returns a policyExists checks if a policy with the given namespace/name is already counted.\n// This is a helper method that must only be called while holding mu.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) newCount, c.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog.Debug(\"Policy counted in namespace\")\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// onPolicyDelete handles policy deletion events.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sync\"\n\n\t\"github.com/sirupsen/logrus\"\n\n\tcilium_v2 log = logging.DefaultLogger.WithField(logfields.LogSubsys, \"policy-quota\")\n\n// PolicyQuotaController enforces per-namespace limits on the number of\n// CiliumNetworkPolicy resources.\ntype PolicyQuotaController struct {\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger\n\n\t// Resource watching CiliumNetworkPolicy objects\n\tcnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]\n\n\t// Maximum number of policies allowed per namespace\n\tmaxPerNamespace int\n\n\t// Thread-safe structures for tracking policies\n\tmu           sync.RWMutex\n\tpolicyCounts map[string]int           // namespace -> count\n\tpolicyKeys   map[string]map[string]bool // namespace -> policyName -> exists\n}\n\n// NewPolicyQuotaController creates a new PolicyQuotaController.\nfunc NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tcnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tlogger:          log,\n\t\tcnpResource:     cnpResource,\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace: maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tpolicyCounts:    make(map[string]int),\n\t\tpolicyKeys:      make(map[string]map[string]bool),\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run starts the controller event loop.\n// It watches for CiliumNetworkPolicy changes and updates internal quota tracking.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n\tscopedLog := c.logger.WithField(logfields.Controller, \"PolicyQuotaController\")\n\tscopedLog.Info(\"Starting PolicyQuotaController\")\n\n\teventChan := c.cnpResource.Events(ctx)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\tscopedLog.Info(\"Stopping PolicyQuotaController\")\n\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-eventChan:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t// Channel closed\n\t\t\t\tscopedLog.Info(\"PolicyQuotaController event channel closed\")\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Handle the event based on its kind\n\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\t// Initial sync complete\n\t\t\t\tscopedLog.Debug(\"Initial policy list sync complete\")\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\terr = c.onPolicyUpsert(event.Object)\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\terr = c.onPolicyDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Mark the event as processed\n\t\t\t// If err is not nil, the event will be retried\n\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// onPolicyUpsert handles policy creation/update events.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyUpsert(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tnamespace := policy.GetNamespace()\n\tname := policy.GetName()\n\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t// Initialize namespace tracking if needed\n\tif _, exists := c.policyKeys[namespace]; !exists {\n\t\tc.policyKeys[namespace] = make(map[string]bool)\n\t}\n\n\t// Only increment if this is a new policy (not previously seen)\n\tif !c.policyKeys[namespace][name] {\n\t\tc.policyKeys[namespace][name] = true\n\t\tc.policyCounts[namespace]++\n\t}\n\n\tnewCount := c.policyCounts[namespace]\n\n\tscopedLog := c.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Controller: \"PolicyQuotaController\",\n\t\t\"namespace\":         namespace,\n\t\t\"policy\":            name,\n\t\t\"count\":             newCount,\n\t\t\"max\":               c.maxPerNamespace,\n\t})\n\n\tif newCount > c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\tscopedLog.Warn(\"Policy quota exceeded for namespace\")\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"policy quota exceeded: namespace %s has %d policies, max is %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, newCount, c.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog.Debug(\"Policy counted in namespace\")\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// onPolicyDelete handles policy deletion events.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyDelete(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tnamespace := policy.GetNamespace()\n\tname := policy.GetName()\n\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tif count, exists := c.policyCounts[namespace]; exists && count > 0 {\n\t\tc.policyCounts[namespace]--\n\t\tif c.policyCounts[namespace] == 0 {\n\t\t\tdelete(c.policyCounts, namespace)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tc.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Controller: \"PolicyQuotaController\",\n\t\t\"namespace\":         namespace,\n\t\t\"policy\":            name,\n\t\t\"count\":             c.policyCounts[namespace],\n\t}).Debug(\"Policy removed from namespace count\")\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// CheckQuota returns an error if the namespace has exceeded its policy quota.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tcount := c.policyCounts[namespace]\n\tc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif count >= c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"policy quota exceeded: namespace %s has %d policies, max is %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, count, c.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GetPolicyCounts returns a snapshot of policy counts per namespace.\n// This is primarily for testing purposes.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) GetPolicyCounts() map[string]int {\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer c.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\t// Return a copy to prevent external modification\n\tcounts := make(map[string]int, len(c.policyCounts))\n\tfor ns, log = logging.DefaultLogger.WithField(logfields.LogSubsys, \"policy-quota\")\n\n// PolicyQuotaController enforces per-namespace limits on the number of\n// CiliumNetworkPolicy resources.\ntype PolicyQuotaController struct {\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger\n\n\t// Resource watching CiliumNetworkPolicy objects\n\tcnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]\n\n\t// Maximum number of policies allowed per namespace\n\tmaxPerNamespace int\n\n\t// Thread-safe structures for tracking policies\n\tmu           sync.RWMutex\n\tpolicyCounts map[string]int           // namespace NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tcnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tlogger: starts the controller event loop.\n// It watches for CiliumNetworkPolicy changes and updates internal quota tracking.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n\tscopedLog := c.logger.WithField(logfields.Controller, \"PolicyQuotaController\")\n\tscopedLog.Info(\"Starting PolicyQuotaController\")\n\n\teventChan := c.cnpResource.Events(ctx)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase closed\n\t\t\t\tscopedLog.Info(\"PolicyQuotaController event channel closed\")\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Handle the event based on its kind\n\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\t// Initial sync complete\n\t\t\t\tscopedLog.Debug(\"Initial policy list sync complete\")\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\terr = c.onPolicyUpsert(event.Object)\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\terr = c.onPolicyDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Mark the event as processed\n\t\t\t// If err is not nil, the event will be retried\n\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// onPolicyUpsert handles policy creation/update events.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyUpsert(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tnamespace := policy.GetNamespace()\n\tname := policy.GetName()\n\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t// Initialize namespace tracking if needed\n\tif _, exists := c.policyKeys[namespace]; !exists {\n\t\tc.policyKeys[namespace] = make(map[string]bool)\n\t}\n\n\t// Only increment if this is a new policy (not previously seen)\n\tif !c.policyKeys[namespace][name] {\n\t\tc.policyKeys[namespace][name] = true\n\t\tc.policyCounts[namespace]++\n\t}\n\n\tnewCount := c.policyCounts[namespace]\n\n\tscopedLog := newCount,\n\t\t\"max\":               c.maxPerNamespace,\n\t})\n\n\tif newCount > c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\tscopedLog.Warn(\"Policy quota exceeded for namespace\")\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"policy quota exceeded: namespace %s has %d policies, max is %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, newCount, c.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog.Debug(\"Policy counted in namespace\")\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// onPolicyDelete handles policy deletion events.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyDelete(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tnamespace := policy.GetNamespace()\n\tname := policy.GetName()\n\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t// Remove from policy key cache\n\tif nsKeys, exists := c.policyKeys[namespace]; exists {\n\t\tdelete(nsKeys, name)\n\t\tif len(nsKeys) == 0 {\n\t\t\tdelete(c.policyKeys, namespace)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Decrement count\n\tif count, exists := c.policyCounts[namespace]; exists && count > 0 {\n\t\tc.policyCounts[namespace]--\n\t\tif c.policyCounts[namespace] == 0 {\n\t\t\tdelete(c.policyCounts, namespace)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tc.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Controller: \"PolicyQuotaController\",\n\t\t\"namespace\":         namespace,\n\t\t\"policy\":            name,\n\t\t\"count\":             c.policyCounts[namespace],\n\t}).Debug(\"Policy removed from namespace count\")\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// CheckQuota returns an error if the namespace has exceeded its policy quota.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tcount := c.policyCounts[namespace]\n\tc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif count >= c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"policy quota exceeded: namespace %s has %d policies, max is %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, count, c.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GetPolicyCounts returns a snapshot of policy counts per namespace.\n// This is primarily for testing purposes.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) GetPolicyCounts() map[string]int {\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer c.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\t// Return a copy to prevent external modification\n\tcounts := make(map[string]int, len(c.policyCounts))\n\tfor ns, count := range c.policyCounts {\n\t\tcounts[ns] = count\n\t}\n\treturn counts\n}\n",

type CiliumPolicyQuota struct {
	// +deepequal-gen=false
	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
	// +deepequal-gen=false
	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata"`

	// Spec is the specification for the CiliumPolicyQuota.
	Spec CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
}

	metav1.ListMeta `json:"metadata"`

	// Items is a list of CiliumPolicyQuota.
	Items []CiliumPolicyQuota `json:"items"`
}

	// +kubebuilder:validation:Required
	// +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1

}

// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package quota

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"sync"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"

	cilium_v2 "github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/resource"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields"
)

var log = logging.DefaultLogger.WithField(logfields.LogSubsys, "policy-quota")

// PolicyQuotaController enforces per-namespace limits on the number of
// CiliumNetworkPolicy resources.
type PolicyQuotaController struct {
	logger logrus.FieldLogger

	// Resource watching CiliumNetworkPolicy objects
	cnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]

	// Maximum number of policies allowed per namespace
	maxPerNamespace int

	// Thread-safe map tracking policy counts per namespace
	mu         sync.RWMutex
	policyCounts map[string]int
}

// NewPolicyQuotaController creates a new PolicyQuotaController.
func NewPolicyQuotaController(
	cnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],
	maxPerNamespace int,
) *PolicyQuotaController {
	return &PolicyQuotaController{
		logger:          log,
		cnpResource:     cnpResource,
		maxPerNamespace: maxPerNamespace,
		policyCounts:    make(map[string]int),
	}
}

// Run starts the controller event loop.
// It watches for CiliumNetworkPolicy changes and updates internal quota tracking.
func (c *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) error {
	scopedLog := c.logger.WithField(logfields.Controller, "PolicyQuotaController")
	scopedLog.Info("Starting PolicyQuotaController")

	eventChan := c.cnpResource.Events(ctx)

	for {
		select {
		case <-ctx.Done():
			scopedLog.Info("Stopping PolicyQuotaController")
			return ctx.Err()

		case event, ok := <-eventChan:
			if 
... (truncated)

	events chan resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]
}

	return m.events
}

// SendEvent is a helper to send events through the mock resource
func (m *MockResource) SendEvent(event resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]) {
	m.events <- event
}

	close(m.events)
}

8. EDIT /workspace/pkg/policy/quota/controller.go
Before
// onPolicyUpsert handles policy creation/update events.
func (c *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyUpsert(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {
	namespace := policy.GetNamespace()
	name := policy.GetName()

	c.mu.Lock()
	defer c.mu.Unlock()

	// Check if this is a new policy
	oldCount := c.policyCounts[namespace]

	// Only increment if the policy wasn't already counted
	// (we detect this by checking if it's a new entry for this namespace)
	if oldCount == 0 || !c.policyExists(namespace, name) {
		c.policyCounts[namespace]++
	}

	newCount := c.policyCounts[namespace]

	scopedLog := c.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{
		logfields.Controller: "PolicyQuotaController",
		"namespace":         namespace,
		"policy":            name,
		"count":             newCount,
		"max":               c.maxPerNamespace,
	})

	if newCount > c.maxPerNamespace {
		scopedLog.Warn("Policy quota exceeded for namespace")
		return fmt.Errorf("policy quota exceeded: namespace %s has %d policies, max is %d",
			namespace, newCount, c.maxPerNamespace)
	}

	scopedLog.Debug("Policy counted in namespace")
	return nil
}
After
// onPolicyUpsert handles policy creation/update events.
func (c *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyUpsert(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {
	namespace := policy.GetNamespace()
	name := policy.GetName()

	c.mu.Lock()
	defer c.mu.Unlock()

	// Initialize namespace tracking if needed
	if _, exists := c.policyKeys[namespace]; !exists {
		c.policyKeys[namespace] = make(map[string]bool)
	}

	// Only increment if this is a new policy (not previously seen)
	if !c.policyKeys[namespace][name] {
		c.policyKeys[namespace][name] = true
		c.policyCounts[namespace]++
	}

	newCount := c.policyCounts[namespace]

	scopedLog := c.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{
		logfields.Controller: "PolicyQuotaController",
		"namespace":         namespace,
		"policy":            name,
		"count":             newCount,
		"max":               c.maxPerNamespace,
	})

	if newCount > c.maxPerNamespace {
		scopedLog.Warn("Policy quota exceeded for namespace")
		return fmt.Errorf("policy quota exceeded: namespace %s has %d policies, max is %d",
			namespace, newCount, c.maxPerNamespace)
	}

	scopedLog.Debug("Policy counted in namespace")
	return nil
}
9. EDIT /workspace/pkg/policy/quota/controller.go
Before
// onPolicyDelete handles policy deletion events.
func (c *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyDelete(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {
	namespace := policy.GetNamespace()
	name := policy.GetName()

	c.mu.Lock()
	defer c.mu.Unlock()

	if count, exists := c.policyCounts[namespace]; exists && count > 0 {
		c.policyCounts[namespace]--
		if c.policyCounts[namespace] == 0 {
			delete(c.policyCounts, namespace)
		}
	}

	c.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{
		logfields.Controller: "PolicyQuotaController",
		"namespace":         namespace,
		"policy":            name,
		"count":             c.policyCounts[namespace],
	}).Debug("Policy removed from namespace count")

	return nil
}
After
// onPolicyDelete handles policy deletion events.
func (c *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyDelete(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {
	namespace := policy.GetNamespace()
	name := policy.GetName()

	c.mu.Lock()
	defer c.mu.Unlock()

	// Remove from policy key cache
	if nsKeys, exists := c.policyKeys[namespace]; exists {
		delete(nsKeys, name)
		if len(nsKeys) == 0 {
			delete(c.policyKeys, namespace)
		}
	}

	// Decrement count
	if count, exists := c.policyCounts[namespace]; exists && count > 0 {
		c.policyCounts[namespace]--
		if c.policyCounts[namespace] == 0 {
			delete(c.policyCounts, namespace)
		}
	}

	c.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{
		logfields.Controller: "PolicyQuotaController",
		"namespace":         namespace,
		"policy":            name,
		"count":             c.policyCounts[namespace],
	}).Debug("Policy removed from namespace count")

	return nil
}

Before
// policyExists checks if a policy with the given namespace/name is already counted.
// This is a helper method that must only be called while holding mu.
func (c *PolicyQuotaController) policyExists(namespace, name string) bool {
	// In a real implementation, this would check against an actual policy store.
	// For now, we track by incrementing on upsert and decrementing on delete.
	// Since we're called only during upsert, we assume the count is accurate.
	return true
}
After
11. EDIT /workspace/pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go
Before
func TestPolicyQuotaControllerUpsertEvent(t *testing.T) {
	mockResource := newMockResource()
	controller := NewPolicyQuotaController(mockResource, 3)

	// Add policies in the "default" namespace
	for i := 1; i <= 3; i++ {
		policy := newTestPolicy("default", "policy-"+string(rune('0'+i)))
		err := controller.onPolicyUpsert(policy)
		assert.NoError(t, err, "unexpected error on upsert %d", i)
	}

	// Verify count
	counts := controller.GetPolicyCounts()
	assert.Equal(t, 3, counts["default"])

	// Try to add 4th policy (should fail)
	policy4 := newTestPolicy("default", "policy-4")
	err := controller.onPolicyUpsert(policy4)
	assert.Error(t, err, "expected error when quota exceeded")

	// Verify count is updated even though it exceeded quota
	counts = controller.GetPolicyCounts()
	assert.Equal(t, 4, counts["default"])
}
After
func TestPolicyQuotaControllerUpsertEvent(t *testing.T) {
	mockResource := newMockResource()
	controller := NewPolicyQuotaController(mockResource, 3)

	// Add policies in the "default" namespace
	for i := 1; i <= 3; i++ {
		policy := newTestPolicy("default", "policy-"+string(rune('0'+i)))
		err := controller.onPolicyUpsert(policy)
		assert.NoError(t, err, "unexpected error on upsert %d", i)
	}

	// Verify count
	counts := controller.GetPolicyCounts()
	assert.Equal(t, 3, counts["default"])

	// Try to add 4th policy (should fail)
	policy4 := newTestPolicy("default", "policy-4")
	err := controller.onPolicyUpsert(policy4)
	assert.Error(t, err, "expected error when quota exceeded")

	// Verify count is updated even though it exceeded quota
	counts = controller.GetPolicyCounts()
	assert.Equal(t, 4, counts["default"])

	// Verify upserting the same policy again doesn't increment count
	err = controller.onPolicyUpsert(policy4)
	assert.Error(t, err, "expected error when quota exceeded")
	counts = controller.GetPolicyCounts()
	assert.Equal(t, 4, counts["default"], "count should remain same for duplicate upsert")
}
